function dist(e, t) {
	return Math.sqrt(Math.pow(t.y - e[2], 2) + Math.pow(t.x - e[1], 2))
}

function isElementVisible(e) {
	return null !== e.offsetParent
}

function toRad(e) {
	return .01745329251 * e
}

function dist(e, t) {
	return Math.sqrt(Math.pow(t.y - e[2], 2) + Math.pow(t.x - e[1], 2))
}

function animate(e, t) {
	let n, o = "";
	n = e ? "NextGen" : "Storm", e && (n = (n = n.padStart((30 - n.length) / 2 + n.length))
		.padEnd(30));
	let r = 0;
	for(let e = 0; e < n.length; e++) 1 == Math.floor(Math.random() * t) && "-" != n.charAt(e) && r < 2 && " " != n.charAt(e) ? (o += ".", r++) : o += n.charAt(e);
	return o
}

			var h, u;
			this.objects = t, this.grids = {}, this.updateObjects = [];
			var f = l.mapScale / l.colGrid;
			this.setObjectGrids = function (e) {
				for(var t = Math.min(l.mapScale, Math.max(0, e.x)), n = Math.min(l.mapScale, Math.max(0, e.y)), o = 0; o < l.colGrid; ++o) {
					h = o * f;
